<h1 _ngcontent-wku-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.account.appAccount (应用账号管理)"> @ohos.account.appAccount (应用账号管理) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-wku-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供应用账号信息的添加、删除、修改和查询基础能力，并支持应用间鉴权和分布式数据同步功能。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.AppAccount</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th <p>开启或禁止指定应用账号的数据同步功能。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.DISTRIBUTED_DATASYNC</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.AppAccount</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">auth<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" string, owner: string, authType: string, callback: AuthCallback): void</p>     <p>对应用账号进行鉴权以获取授权令牌。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.AppAccount</p> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调对象，返回鉴权结果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a <p>对应用账号进行鉴权以获取授权令牌。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.AppAccount</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div id="selectaccountsbyoptions9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">selectAccountsByOptions<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="selectaccountsbyoptions9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>selectAccountsByOptions(options: SelectAccountsOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Array&lt;AppAccountInfo&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据选项选择调用方可访问的账号列表。使用callback异步回调。如果选项中包含标签约束，则该方法依赖目标应用的认证器提供标签检查的能力。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.AppAccount</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-appaccount#selectaccountsoptions9">SelectAccountsOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">选择账号的选项。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当根据选项选择请求方可访问的账号列表时，err为null，data为可访问的账号信息对象；否则为错误对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> id="onchangedeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">on('change')<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onchangedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>on(type: 'change', owners: Array&lt;string&gt;, callback: Callback&lt;Array&lt;AppAccountInfo&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>订阅指定应用的账号信息变更事件。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 9开始废弃。建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-appaccount#onaccountchange9">on('accountChange')</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.AppAccount</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.96.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.96.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.96.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.96.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">'change'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">事件回调类型，支持的事件为'change'，当账号所有者更新账号信息时，触发该事件。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">owners</td>         <td class="cellrowborder"
